The 13 topics jointly imply a large interdependent migration set: DNT backfill + Conversation column drop, Application/Answer re-keying from conversation to customer scope (unique-constraint changes), Quote.applicationId 1:1 resolution + QuoteStatus/ApplicationStatus/PaymentStatus/PolicyStatus enum extensions (CANCELLED, REFERRED, LAPSED, ABANDONED), new tables (DntSession, DisclosureAck, Document, ProductContent, schedule/inbox), and dead-config cleanup (Workflow*/skill-pack gating, phantom seed tools). Nobody owns ordering, backfill correctness, or deploy-atomicity hazards — most acutely: accept_quote must stop creating Policy in the SAME deploy that payments starts issuing it, or there is a window with either zero or two policy-creation paths. Depends on: all topics; most tightly quote-lifecycle, payments, dnt-sessions, application-lifecycle.

### M10. Resilience/outage semantics: infra-failure taxonomy and retry policy

The @contract scenario 'A tool/endpoint outage degrades gracefully' (zeno_workflow.feature:68-71) requires distinguishing infrastructure failure from business rejection, but the catalog's 14-value taxonomy contains NO infra-failure/timeout/unavailable value — commit-envelope flags the conflation but its envelope question doesn't decide outage representation, retry policy, circuit-breaker behavior, payment-provider-down handling, or degraded-mode exposure (does a tool whose backend is down appear in blocked_actions, and with what reason?). Depends on: commit-envelope, legality-engine, payments, tool-mapping.

### M11. Canonical eligibility rule representation (one source, three evaluation points)

Three topics each place eligibility evaluation somewhere — product-data (engine-computed verdict in derived state at discovery), questionnaire-consequences (synchronous edge-scoped recheck on answers), quote-lifecycle (typed decision inside generate_quote) — but no topic owns the single rule source they must share. Today Product.eligibility Json is never evaluated and AddonPricingRule age bands silently price at 0 on no-match. If product-data authors eligibility_bounds as content while generate_quote evaluates Product.eligibility, the rules triplicate exactly like the prices product-data flags. Needs one owner for the rule schema, its evaluation function, and the guarantee that the discovery signal, the recheck, and the final gate are the same predicate at different data-completeness levels. Depends on: product-data, questionnaire-consequences, quote-lifecycle, legality-engine.

### M12. Skill-pack / prompt-content layer fate beyond gating

legality-engine retires SkillPack.allowedTools as a GATING source and phase-model rebuilds prompt sections, but skill packs also carry sales playbooks/scripts (product-data flags hardcoded prices in defaultPlaybook), pack activation is dead (orchestrator.ts:597 recommendedSlugs=[]), and POST_SALE packs are dead config with phantom tools. No topic decides whether the pack system survives as a prompt-content mechanism, who selects packs per turn after the reasoning gate's retirement, or whether packs are deleted outright — leaving a dangling subsystem after the gating role is removed. Depends on: legality-engine, phase-model, product-data, policy-post-sale.

### M13. Discovery conversational policy preservation through the prompt rework (out-of-scope deflection, pushback-without-pressure)

'Out-of-scope topics are declined politely' (feature:80-82) and 'Consultative pushback without pressure' (feature:113-116) are implemented today purely in prompt sections (the catalog-overview section and guardrails that fixed the four documented conversational pathologies). phase-model's recommended per-(phase,subphase) sections rework rebuilds exactly that prompt surface, and testing-bdd only VERIFIES the behaviors (judge-quarantined). No topic owns carrying the behavioral content through the rework — a silent regression channel for already-fixed pathologies. Depends on: phase-model, testing-bdd.

### M14. Multiple candidate products explored in parallel (@discovery backlog)

Backlog item (zeno_workflow.feature:453). Conversation.candidateProductId is a single pointer (prisma/schema.prisma:304) and the catalog declares candidate_product the SOLE owner of product-in-focus. No topic decides whether parallel candidates are supported, modeled (candidate set vs single + comparison reads), or explicitly ruled out — and compare_products already exists as a tool that sits outside the candidate model. With one real product this is dormant, but the candidate-SSOT regression guard (feature:444-447) makes the decision normative. Depends on: product-data, tool-mapping, application-lifecycle.

### M15. Answer freshness/expiry and duplicate-existing-policy detection (@questionnaire backlog)

Backlog item (zeno_workflow.feature:455). No topic question covers staleness of answers in a resumed application (an application resumed weeks later carries possibly stale health/income declarations — interacts with application-lifecycle's cross-conversation resume and prefill-as-proposals), nor detecting that the customer already holds an equivalent policy (requires the CNP equality lookup identity flags as impossible today due to random-IV encryption — blind index needed — but no topic owns the duplicate-policy business rule itself). Depends on: questionnaire-consequences, application-lifecycle, identity, policy-post-sale.

### M16. Dunning, grace period, and lapse rules (@payment backlog)

Backlog item 'installment failure after issuance; grace / lapse' (zeno_workflow.feature:457). payments owns the schedule model and policy-post-sale adds the LAPSED status, but neither has a question for the actual rules: grace-period length, retry cadence for failed installments, customer notification, reinstatement after lapse, and pro-rata/refund interaction. The two topics' recommendations bound the data model but the policy logic that connects 'installment failed' to 'policy LAPSED' is unowned. Depends on: payments, policy-post-sale, operator surfaces (see above).

### Critic notes

SPEC-INTERNAL INCONSISTENCIES / UNIMPLEMENTABLE-AS-WRITTEN (zeno_tool_catalog.md + zeno_workflow.feature):
1. The 14-value consequence taxonomy has no infrastructure-failure/timeout value, yet the @contract outage scenario (feature:68-71) requires distinguishing outage from business rejection; and the quote-generation Examples row 'rejected | pending_external_check' (feature:329) models a PENDING state as a rejection — the taxonomy has no pending/in-progress value, and under 'issuing a quote completes the application', the spec never says what a rejected/referred generate_quote leaves behind (is the application still incomplete and answer-modifiable? can generate_quote be retried after the external check clears?). Load-bearing and undefined.
2. referred (manual underwriting) has no return path anywhere in the catalog: no operator tool, no state for 'referred pending', no mechanism for an underwriter decision to re-enter the engine and resume the customer. The consequence exists; its resolution does not.
3. DNT 'flat (no branching, no dependents)' (catalog assumption 3, feature:136) contradicts products_covered by subtype: get_dnt_state reports coverage per type 'home, car, life-simple, or life-with-investment' (feature:144-145), which requires either subtype-dependent question sets (= branching; the seeds gate life_financial/investment/sustainability groups on DNT_LIFE_SUBTYPE) or asking every customer all questions and deriving coverage some unspecified way. dnt-sessions' 'visibility-only branching' resolution is a deviation from the spec text, not a reading of it.
4. The frozen-snapshot assumption ('application freezes a snapshot of candidate at creation', set_application(product_id, addon_ids[])) contradicts the eligibility_recheck consequence: bd_medical-style underwriting answers can render a frozen addon ineligible mid-questionnaire, so the addon set CANNOT be immutable from creation. The panel's 'freeze product only' + select_coverage resolves this, but the catalog as written is internally inconsistent.
5. Catalog tool inputs carry caller-supplied identity (start_dnt_session(user_id), get_customer_info(session/identity), get_application_list(identity), get_open_items(identity)) — contradicting the architecture contract that the agent has no privileged access and the swap test, and perpetuating the exact spoofable-customerId transport hole the identity topic documents. Identity must be server-resolved from the session, never a tool argument.
6. get_policy_status's status enum (active/lapsed/cancelled) omits paid-but-not-yet-submitted and submitted-awaiting-Allianz states that 'payment module issues the policy' + the manual Allianz SOP require; 'First successful payment issues the policy automatically' (feature:402-405) is unimplementable as 'active' — 'issue' is undefined.
7. Free-look cancellation (request_cancellation terminal in window) necessarily implies a premium refund; the spec contains no refund tool, consequence, or payment-module effect — the terminal consequence is incomplete as specified.
8. @payment exposure is circular for the re-engagement case: get_payment_status/resume_payment are exposed 'in @payment', but a returning customer days later is in a new conversation that the catalog gives no rule for entering @payment; only get_open_items bridges it, and the phase-entry rule is unspecified.
9. The taxonomy table says a consequence is 'returned by every commit' (singular), yet several rows chain two (requires_confirmation -> terminal; requires_confirmation -> advance_phase; advance_phase + application-completion side effect of generate_quote). Whether a commit returns one consequence or an ordered set is unspecified — commit-envelope's outcome+effects[] answers it, but as a spec deviation, not a reading.
10. The catalog hardcodes Stripe ('Stripe owns card entry') but the codebase runs three providers (lib/payments/providers/stripe.ts, payu.ts, mock.ts) with live stripe AND payu webhook routes (app/api/webhooks/), and the PayU webhook has the signature-bypass flaw the payments digest documents. The spec's Stripe-only framing leaves multi-provider settlement semantics out of scope without saying so.
11. modify_dnt_answer is exposed while 'a new or update session is active', but sign_dnt is exposed when the 'session finished' — whether a finished-but-unsigned session still counts as active (i.e., can the customer amend an answer between the finish signal and signing, which the consent-refusal scenario's 'answered session is preserved' makes practically important) is unspecified.
12. resume_application is typed R (read) in the catalog but listed among the questionnaire tools with commit-like placement; today's implementation is a commit (unpauses). Harmless naming issue, but the R/C discipline is the spec's core typing and this row is ambiguous.
VERIFICATION NOTES: all code claims above were checked against the worktree (providers and webhook routes via glob; lib/i18n existence; Conversation.language schema.prisma:277; candidateProductId schema.prisma:304; bilingual Question.text JSON at lib/tools/handlers/application-handlers.ts:116; uiAction vocabulary grep across lib/). I did NOT find any i18n handling for engine-emitted/blocked-reason text, any consent ledger, any suitability mapping from DNT answers to products, or any consumer of the TurnDebug data for assertions — confirmed absent by search, consistent with the panel digests.

---

## Suggested discussion order

The 73 decision points cluster into blocks; within a block, the decisions constrain each other (see the contradiction list) and are best discussed together. One decision point at a time, in this sequence:

### Block A — Architecture spine (everything else keys off these)
1. **T1.D1 + T1.D2 + T1.D4** — where legality lives, how it is enforced, how "exposed when" is expressed.
2. **T2.D1 + T2.D2** — commit envelope shape and the central gateway.
3. **T10.D1 + T10.D2** — target phase enumeration and derived-vs-stored phase. ⚠ Decide jointly with T1.D5 and T2.D1: contradiction #6 demands that advance_phase be literally one computation.

### Block B — Funnel front: identity × DNT × consent (contradictions #1, #2, #7, #12)
4. **T4.D1 + T4.D2 + T5.D1 + T3.D1** — identity tiers, which tier unlocks set_application vs sign_dnt vs accept_quote, DNT ordering (application-first vs DNT-first), DNT scope. This is the product-shaping decision of the whole transformation: how much identity do we demand before a needs analysis?
5. **T3.D5 + T13.D6 + M3** — consent source of truth: fold into sign_dnt vs consent ledger; withdraw_consent semantics. ⚠ Contradiction #2: folding everything into sign_dnt cannot serve non-DNT consents and withdrawal.
6. **T3.D3 + T3.D4 + T3.D6 + T13.D5** — DNT coverage modeling, exact tool surface (the 6-vs-7-tool arithmetic of contradiction #7), flat-vs-visibility-branching, plus contradiction #12 (customer-scoped renewal exposure outside @application).

### Block C — Application core (contradictions #4, #9)
7. **T5.D2 + T5.D3** — the selection gap: where tier/level/addon selection lives and what freezes at set_application.
8. **T6.D1 + T6.D2 + T6.D6** — dependency representation, cascade semantics, planner/applier split. ⚠ Contradiction #4: the dependency graph must span answers AND selection state, or select_coverage owns its own invalidation.
9. **M11 + T11.D4 + T6.D5 + T7.D4** — one canonical eligibility rule source evaluated at three funnel points (discovery signal, mid-questionnaire recheck, generate_quote gate). ⚠ Contradiction #9.
10. **T5.D4 + T5.D5 + T5.D6** — application scoping/multiplicity, prefill-as-proposals, status model.

### Block D — Money and policy (contradictions #3, #5, #11)
11. **T7.D1 + T7.D6** — immutability moment and the narrow accept (no Policy at accept).
12. **T8.D2 + T9.D3 + T9.D2** — policy issuance timing, status machine incl. LAPSED, free-look anchor. ⚠ Contradiction #5: "issued/effective/active" must be defined once across three topics.
13. **T8.D1 + T8.D5 + T7.D3** — schedule model and payment-frequency SSOT. ⚠ Contradiction #3: the schedule record must be the live-frequency truth; Quote.paymentFrequency demotes to acceptance evidence.
14. **T8.D3 + T8.D4** — webhook reconciliation, recovery tool shape (single ensure_payment_session).
15. **T10.D3 + contradiction #11** — conversation terminality: what replaces Conversation.status=COMPLETED.
16. **T7.D2 + T9.D1** — disclosures model and the document registry (DisclosureAck + Document table).

### Block E — Content, surface, post-sale
17. **T11.D1 + T11.D2 + T11.D5** — pricing_examples/eligibility_bounds storage, versioned ProductContent, seed migration.
18. **M12 + M13 + T10.D4** — skill-pack fate beyond gating, preservation of the conversational-pathology fixes through the sections rework.
19. **T13.D1, D2, D3, D4, D7, D8** — residual tool-disposition calls (mostly settled by Blocks B–D; ratify quickly).
20. **T4.D5 + M4** — transport identity (server-resolved session) and the GUI/uiAction swap-test contract.
21. **T9.D4 + T9.D5 + T9.D6 + M5** — Allianz submission visibility, @policy tool surface, post-sale phase derivation, operator/back-office surfaces (referral queue, refund execution).

### Block F — Verification and delivery
22. **T12.D1–D5** — test harness, scenario classification, engine seam, agent-behavior evidence, living-spec traceability.
23. **M8** — TurnDebug/observability extension (the assertion substrate for #22 and the compliance audit trail).
24. **M9** — migration & deploy sequencing (incl. the policy-creation atomicity hazard: accept_quote must stop creating Policy in the same deploy that payments starts issuing it).
25. **Parking lot** — M6 (i18n), M7 (suitability/demands-and-needs engine), M10 (outage taxonomy), M14 (parallel candidates), M15 (answer freshness / duplicate policy), M16 (dunning/grace/lapse rules). Each needs at least an explicit defer decision.

### Spec doc fixes to fold back
The critic found 12 internal inconsistencies in the spec docs themselves (see "Critic notes" above) — e.g. no pending/infra-failure consequence value, referred has no return path, caller-supplied identity in tool inputs violates the spec's own swap test, "first payment issues the policy" is undefined under the manual Allianz SOP. The catalog and .feature should be amended as decisions land, since they are living specs.

---

## Resolved decisions (running log)

### 2026-06-12 — All panel recommendations ratified

The user reviewed the full document and agreed with every ✅ Recommended option as the working direction. Deviations and refinements are logged below as topics get discussed in depth; where a log entry refines a topic, the log entry wins.

### 2026-06-12 — T4 Identity: RESOLVED (with refinements)

Grounding established during discussion: the Allianz submission SOP (`docs/allianz-submission-sop.md`) requires customer data (name, age, CNP, email, phone) + DNT report but **no ID copy** — document verification is Zeno's business rule, not an Allianz requirement. A working magic-link → JWT flow exists (`app/api/auth/magic-link/route.ts`, `app/api/auth/verify/route.ts`) but serves only the dashboard: no claim-and-merge with the anonymous chat customer, no return-to-conversation.

**R1 — Two orthogonal verification kinds.** Channel verification (email/SMS OTP, magic link) = authentication, proves channel ownership, makes the customer durable across devices. Evidence verification (photo ID, car registration, …) = attribute verification, **per-field not per-customer** (an ID verifies cnp/name/DOB; a car registration verifies vehicle attributes). Never collapse the two into one "verified customer" flag.

**R2 — Per-field provenance is the data model** (and the concrete shape of M1 CustomerProfile SSOT): each field carries `declared | verified | conflict` + source + timestamp + evidence-record pointer. Identity **tier is derived** from field states + channel status, never stored.

**R3 — Promotion invariant: the agent requests verification, the engine grants it; verified beats declared.** A customer cannot talk a verified value down; only new evidence or operator override changes verified data. Document flow: `request_document_upload(kind)` → `show_document_upload` uiAction (agent never touches the image, Stripe-card pattern) → system pipeline: store encrypted → extract (OCR/vision allowed — extraction is not a decision) → **deterministic validation** (CNP checksum, extracted-vs-declared match with normalization, document expiry; LLM is never the validator) → fields flip to `verified`, mismatches to `conflict` (agent surfaces). Failed extraction/validation → operator review queue (feeds M5). Validator is provider-pluggable (like payment providers) so real eKYC/liveness can slot in later — v1 is consistency-checking, not liveness.

**R4 — Verification is a mutation event for the consequence engine (T6):** a verified CNP changes derived age → can trigger `eligibility_recheck` / `re_rating` exactly like `modify_answer`.

**R5 — Passwordless only; one challenge primitive.** No passwords ever. One `VerificationChallenge` (hashed code, expiry, attempt limit) presented two ways: 6-digit OTP typed in chat (primary, in-conversation) and magic link (same challenge wrapped in a URL, for out-of-conversation re-engagement). Existing magic-link/JWT code becomes a special case; verifying a channel binds the session to the verified Customer and runs **claim-and-merge** of anonymous artifacts (conversation, DNT, application) instead of redirecting to the dashboard.

**R6 — Gate placement:** soft-offer channel verification at `set_application` ("save your progress" — makes the 365-day customer-scoped DNT durable); **hard gate: verified channel at `accept_quote`**; document requirements are **per-product config** (`verificationRequirements` consumed by the legality engine like eligibility rules), defaulting for `protect` to ID photo at accept / before `initiate_payment`. `requires_identity` consequence carries what is missing (e.g. `{needs: ['verified:cnp']}`).

### 2026-06-12 — T14 Observability layer (new topic): RESOLVED D1–D5

Discussed after T4. Today's chassis: DebugEvent stream → reducer → DebugTurn payload → TurnDebug upsert by traceId (`lib/chat/turn-debug-persistence.ts`, fire-and-forget, failures swallowed by design); drawer renders the same shape; download + replay exist.

**T14.D1 — ✅ RESOLVED: first-class append-only commit ledger** (DomainEvent/CommitRecord table), written transactionally inside the commit gateway (T2.D2): one row per commit attempt — tool, actor (agent|gui|system|operator), envelope outcome + reason, pre/post phase, idempotency disposition, confirm-token lifecycle, verification events, disclosure presentations with content version. TurnDebug references ledger IDs, never duplicates domain truth. Ledger = audit/compliance/test substrate, long-lived; TurnDebug stays droppable.

**T14.D2 — accepted as recommended:** per-turn legality snapshot in TurnDebug (DerivedState + available_actions/blocked_actions with reasons + engine version stamp); replay upgraded to recompute-and-diff (same engine version → diff = bug; new version → diff = reviewable behavioral changelog / shadow replay).

**T14.D3 — accepted as recommended:** runtime invariant monitors from the @contract scenarios (mechanical subset): briefing-integrity check (every briefing-recommended action must be in available_actions — would have caught the live 10-tool regression), executor rejections of non-exposed tools, envelope-missing alarm, idempotent-replay counter, confirm-token expiry rate. Linguistic invariants stay in the test layer (T12 judge-quarantine).

**T14.D4 — ✅ RESOLVED (deviation from recommendation): BOTH viewers from day one** — compliance evidence view (customer-scoped timeline: disclosures+versions, consents, DNT signature, verifications, confirmations) in the admin UI for operators AND surfaced in the debug drawer for developers. Same ledger, two viewers.

**T14.D5 — accepted as recommended:** sensitive-data policy — ledger stores references not values (evidence-record IDs, field names + provenance states, never CNP itself); TurnDebug redaction pass for identity fields; retention split (TurnDebug short-lived/prunable, ledger long-lived per insurance retention); document images never enter either stratum.

**T14.D6 — conversation triage tooling: under discussion** (deterministic checker script + Claude Code skill hybrid proposed).

### 2026-06-12 — T14.D6 Conversation triage tooling: RESOLVED — build LAST (end of Block F)

Agreed design — two layers plus operator instructions:

1. **Layer 1 — deterministic checker** (`scripts/diagnose-conversation.ts` + pure check catalog in `lib/diagnostics/`): loads a conversation's recorded data (TurnDebug payloads, messages; post-transformation: commit ledger + legality snapshots), runs a unit-tested check catalog, outputs findings (checkId, severity, turn, evidence) as table + JSON. Three run modes: single conversation, nightly batch triage queue (`--all --since=N`), and CI over e2e sims (feeds T12). v1 catalog (~12 checks) works on today's data: briefing_tool_not_exposed, tool_call_failed, tool_call_without_result, turn_not_ended, funnel_stalled, phase_regression, state_snapshot_inconsistent, duplicate_turn_debug, anomalies_reported, latency_outlier, repeated_assistant_message, ended_pre_closing. v2 adds envelope/legality checks once T14.D1/D2 land.
2. **Layer 2 — `/diagnose-conversation` Claude Code skill** (`.claude/skills/diagnose-conversation/SKILL.md`): runs Layer 1, treats findings as ground truth (verify-from-source discipline), pulls raw turn payloads + DB rows for flagged turns, root-causes into the codebase (classes: prompt-content / engine-rule / handler-bug / tool-exposure / data-seed / llm-behavior), writes report to `docs/debug-reports/<date>-<id>.md` with what/where(file:line)/why/concrete fix/prevention. **Ratchet rule:** any issue class the checker missed becomes a new deterministic check (test-first) before the investigation closes.
3. **Debugging runbook** (`docs/debugging-conversations.md`): human instructions for the three-level stack — drawer (live) → checker (deterministic CLI) → skill (root-cause report) — including the rule "never diagnose from conversation prose; recorded state is the evidence."

**Sequencing decision (user, 2026-06-12): the script and the skill are created at the END, after everything else is built** — last item of Block F, after M9 (migration/deploy sequencing). Rationale: the check catalog asserts against the final shapes (target phase vocabulary, commit ledger, legality snapshots, new prompt sections); built earlier it would assert against shapes the transformation replaces.

Design-validation note: a throwaway v1 prototype was built and verified during this discussion (26 unit tests green; full suite green except the known instrumentation flake; a live batch run against the dev DB flagged findings in 9/9 recent conversations — including `briefing_tool_not_exposed` hits consistent with the live 10-tool regression). The prototype was then removed per the sequencing decision; the design recorded above is the durable spec and the structure is proven to rebuild quickly at its slot.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #1 (identity tier × DNT ordering × DNT scope): CLEARED

Resolved by T4-R5/R6 + T5.D1 (confirmed by user): no hard identity gate before the needs analysis — `set_application` and `sign_dnt` run on declared data with a soft channel-verification offer at `set_application`; hard verified-channel gate at `accept_quote`; the anonymous customer's Dnt is customer-scoped from the start and claim-and-merge attaches it to the verified identity at latest at acceptance, so the 365-day DNT value is deferred, never lost.

**New build item — per-commit identity-requirements table:** legality-engine input data, one row per commit: minimum identity tier + minimum declared fields (e.g. `generate_quote` → declared + CNP-or-DOB; `accept_quote` → verified channel; `initiate_payment` → verified channel + product-configured documents; earlier commits → anonymous/declared). `requires_identity` consequences read their `needs` payload from this table.

**Spec amendment:** catalog's `set_application … requires_identity` row updated to the tiered model (identity hard-gates acceptance, not application).

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #2 (consent-truth migration): CLEARED — capture ≠ storage

Confirmed by user. Resolution separates consent capture from consent storage:

**New build item — `ConsentEvent` append-only ledger** as the single consent SSOT (kind: gdpr_processing | ai_disclosure | marketing | …; scope; granted/withdrawn; timestamp; source commit). `Customer.gdprConsentAt`/`aiDisclosureAcknowledgedAt` and `Conversation.dntSignedAt`-as-consent-truth are retired via one-shot backfill into ledger rows. Derived consent state (latest grant not superseded by withdrawal) becomes a `DerivedState` field; **the legality engine reads only the derived state** — switched in the SAME coordinated change as the sign_dnt fold (no period with two truths).

**New build item — `withdraw_consent` commit**: appends a withdrawal event; "processing halts" becomes an engine rule (gdpr_processing withdrawn ⇒ all writing commits blocked, reason surfaced). Withdrawal blocks processing, never deletes data — the answered-session-preserved scenario falls out naturally.

**Amendment to T3.D5 / T13.D6:** `sign_dnt` is the sole consent-*capturing* funnel commit (UX unchanged — customer consents once, at signing); internally it appends ConsentEvent rows. Future non-DNT consents append to the same ledger from whatever commit captures them.

Pre-resolves the consent half of M3 (GDPR rights); M3 discussion narrows to data access/erasure.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #3 (payment-frequency SSOT): CLEARED — schedule is live truth

Confirmed by user. Resolution:

1. **Design rule:** PaymentSchedule is the single live-frequency/amounts truth from acceptance onward. `Quote.paymentFrequency` + `acceptedAt` are immutable acceptance evidence — written once at accept, never updated, never re-read for money math.
2. **Build detail (amends T7.D6 + T8.D1):** `accept_quote` creates the PaymentSchedule transactionally (amounts from the same calculateQuote pass as the chosen option). The PAYMENT phase derives from "schedule exists and isn't settled" (feeds T10.D3); `advance_phase → @payment` corresponds to this real state change.
3. **Design rule:** all payment reads and charges (`get_payment_status`, ensure-payment-session amounts, future dunning) source amounts exclusively from the schedule; `change_payment_option` re-rates by regenerating schedule rows via the quote engine, never mutating the Quote.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #4 (selection-validity ownership): CLEARED — one graph, two node kinds

Confirmed by user. Resolution:

1. **Design decision:** the dependency graph spans both domains with typed nodes — `answer:<questionCode>` and `selection:<facet>` (tier|level|addon); edge kinds (visibility, validity, eligibility) apply across both. Canonical edges become first-class: `selection:level` validity-depends-on `selection:tier`; `bd_medical` group visibility-depends-on `selection:addon`; `selection:addon` eligibility-depends-on `answer:bd_*`.
2. The consequence planner (T6.D6) consumes mutation events from BOTH `modify_answer`-class commits and `select_coverage`; one transactional applier executes through the commit gateway. Tier change ⇒ re_rating + cascade_invalidate of invalid level; addon toggle ⇒ cascade_expand/questions_removed of bd_medical.
3. **Invariant preserved:** `select_coverage` is the sole writer of selection state; planner computes, applier executes via the commit path.
4. **Design rule:** bd_medical-driven addon ineligibility is applied deterministically — applier removes the addon, commit returns `eligibility_recheck` with reason, agent must surface it. Never silent, never LLM-judged.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #5 (policy issuance semantics): CLEARED — one definitional table

Confirmed by user. The policy lifecycle is defined once, jointly owned by T7/T8/T9:

| Moment | Effect | Actor | Term |
|---|---|---|---|
| accept_quote | NO Policy; PaymentSchedule created (per contradiction #3) | engine | accepted |
| First successful payment (T8.D3 inbox) | Policy created in PENDING_SUBMISSION, issuedAt stamped | payment module (system; no agent tool) | **issued** |
| SOP transmit | PENDING_SUBMISSION → SUBMITTED | operator | submitted |
| Allianz confirm + number | SUBMITTED → ACTIVE; effectiveFrom set; **freeLookEndsAt frozen = activation + product-configured window** | operator | **active/effective** |
| Allianz rejection pre-activation, or free-look cancellation | → CANCELLED + **automatic full refund executed by payment module** | operator triggers / engine executes | cancelled |
| Installment-failure rules | → LAPSED | deferred to M16 | lapsed |

1. **Design rule:** agent language is engine-gated — never claims in-force before ACTIVE; between payment and activation: "paid, being processed".
2. **New build item — refund execution** as a payment-module system effect with two triggers (free-look request_cancellation; pre-activation cancellation incl. Allianz rejection). Brings PaymentStatus.REFUNDED to life; closes spec hole (free-look implied a refund the spec never provided).
3. **Spec amendments:** .feature "first payment issues the policy automatically" → issue = create-in-PENDING_SUBMISSION; catalog get_policy_status enum += pending_submission, submitted; request_cancellation gains the refund effect.
4. Free-look anchor (activation) + window length are product config, **flagged for legal/compliance confirmation**.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #6 (single advance_phase computation): CLEARED — design constraint

Confirmed by user. Design constraint on Block A (no new build item; welds T1/T2/T10 into one delivery unit):

1. **One function `deriveAndExpose(snapshot) → {derivedState, availableActions, blockedActions}`** is the only code that computes phase or exposure — it is also the pure decision core T12.D3 requires.
2. **The commit gateway is the sole post-commit call site**: apply in transaction → deriveAndExpose on post-state → the envelope's `advance_phase` effect IS the pre/post delta of that call (never handler-asserted); the post-call exposure set drives the next tool round.
3. **Enumerated consumers:** turn start, commit gateway, get_current_state/state injection, T14.D2 recompute-and-diff replay. Meta-test closure rule (T12.D5): no other module may emit a Phase value — guards against a second implementation.
4. TurnDebug legality snapshots record pre+post derivations per commit round, making the replay diff and the briefing-integrity monitor diffs of the same function's outputs.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #7 (DNT tool-surface arithmetic): CLEARED — pinned 6-tool surface

Confirmed by user. The exact DNT surface (amends T3.D4 + T13.D5 jointly):

Reads (3): **get_dnt_state** (validity, product-types covered, expiry, PLUS active-session summary — absorbs get_dnt_session_details; the one-active-session invariant makes this unambiguous), **get_dnt_questions** (preview, no session), **get_dnt_next_question** (active session).
Commits (3): **open_dnt_session** (engine decides new vs update from DNT state — no separate update_dnt; error-with-active-id if a session is active), **write_dnt_answer** (first write or change — flat semantics make a separate modify pointless), **sign_dnt** (consent-capture commit per contradiction #2).

**Spec amendment:** catalog DNT table 9 → 6 tools. Exposure predicates for the six are settled under contradiction #12 (customer-scoped, not @application-only).

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #8 (idempotency × confirm-token ordering): CLEARED — pinned gateway sequence

Confirmed by user. The commit gateway's check order is pinned (design constraint on T2):

1. Resolve actor (server-resolved session, T4.D5)
2. **Idempotency replay detection FIRST** — replay = same tool + same target + same material-args hash; if already applied, return the ORIGINAL outcome envelope from the commit ledger (T14.D1 row schema gains: args hash + stored outcome). Replay-first holds even if the action is now blocked — the block reflects post-application state.
3. Legality (deriveAndExpose) — blocked ⇒ rejected with engine reason; never reaches token logic
4. Confirm token (requires_confirmation commits only): absent → requires_confirmation + token fingerprinting current state; stale/mismatched → RE-ISSUE with fresh fingerprint (not hard reject); valid → proceed
5. Domain validation of args
6. Transactional apply (per-conversation advisory lock, T2.D5) + ledger row in same transaction
7. deriveAndExpose post-state → envelope with advance_phase delta (per contradiction #6)

**Rule:** conflicting resubmit (same target, different material args after success) is NOT a replay → rejected(already_applied), never a second effect, never a silent overwrite.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #9 (eligibility triple-implementation): CLEARED — canonical eligibility module (resolves M11)

Confirmed by user.

1. **New build item — canonical eligibility module:** `Product.eligibility` formalized into a typed, versioned rule schema (facts: age, smoker, bd_* answers…; operators; bounds) + ONE pure function `evaluateEligibility(rules, knownFacts) → {verdict: eligible|ineligible|unknown, failedRules:[{rule,reason}], missingFacts:[]}` — three-valued because early-funnel facts are partial; lives in the T12.D3 pure decision core.
2. **Design constraint:** exactly three call points — discovery verdict in DerivedState (T11.D4), dependency-graph eligibility-edge recheck (T6.D5), generate_quote final gate (T7.D4, its rejected(reason) values = the same failedRules reasons). Nothing else evaluates eligibility.
3. **Presentation drift killed:** numeric eligibility_bounds shown in discovery are DERIVED from the rules; only narrative is authored (amends T11.D1 along its own derive-numbers/author-narrative line).
4. **Folded bug fix:** AddonPricingRule age-band no-match becomes an ineligibility fact — never a silent price 0.

M11 is resolved by this item.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #10 (phase-rename sequencing): CLEARED — pinned vocabulary + atomic A1 package

Confirmed by user, including the concrete target enumeration:

**Pinned phase vocabulary:** `Phase = DISCOVERY | APPLICATION | QUOTE | PAYMENT | POLICY`; `Subphase` (APPLICATION only) `= DNT | QUESTIONNAIRE | QUOTE_GENERATION`.
Old-stage fates: DISCOVERY replaced (absorbs candidate work from SELECTION); SELECTION eliminated (candidate→DISCOVERY, tier/level→select_coverage in APPLICATION); CONSENT eliminated (capture at sign_dnt); QUESTIONNAIRE demoted to subphase; old QUOTE("ready to generate")→QUOTE_GENERATION subphase, new QUOTE = issued-quote review; CLOSING split into PAYMENT and POLICY.
Derivation predicates: DISCOVERY = no open application; APPLICATION/DNT = open app + no valid customer-scoped DNT covering product type (valid-DNT returners skip the subphase by predicate); APPLICATION/QUESTIONNAIRE = valid DNT + answers/selection incomplete (selection incompleteness is a generate_quote blocked-reason, NOT a subphase); APPLICATION/QUOTE_GENERATION = complete, no issued quote; QUOTE = ISSUED quote exists; PAYMENT = accepted quote + schedule, no Policy row; POLICY = Policy exists, derived customer-scoped (T9.D6).

**Sequencing constraint — A1 is one atomic work package:** target enum + deriveAndExpose authored against it from day one + retirement of BOTH old vocabularies (6-value derive-state names and 3-value phase.ts/compliance keying at orchestrator.ts:651) + compliance re-keyed + taxonomy-closure meta-test lands with the enum + existing tests migrated. **Plan rule: no new code is ever authored against old phase names.** Historical TurnTrace/TurnDebug phase strings get tolerant read-only mapping; no data rewrite.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #11 (conversation terminality): CLEARED — conversations are channels

Confirmed by user. Conversation lifecycle fully decoupled from funnel state:

1. **Design decision:** `Conversation.status` carries zero funnel semantics; enum simplifies to `ACTIVE | ARCHIVED` (COMPLETED/ABANDONED retired; historical rows mapped read-only). Nothing in the funnel ever sets conversation status — funnel truth lives in domain entities, phase is derived.
2. **Small build item:** inactivity archival sweep (config window) + reactivate-on-turn; **remove the orchestrator hard-reject** (orchestrator.ts:351-353) — safe because legality now derives from engine state, not conversation status; a turn on an old conversation gets exposure from current customer-scoped state by construction. Lands together with T7.D6 narrow accept (no window where conversations can never close).
3. **Rule:** returning-user entry is channel-indifferent (new or reactivated conversation behave identically; get_open_items surfaces pending work). Analytics "completion" = derived domain events (quote accepted, policy issued), never conversation status.

### 2026-06-12 — Contradiction #12 (DNT exposure scope): CLEARED — predicates over the full snapshot

Confirmed by user.

1. **Design rule (refines T1.D4):** exposure predicates range over the FULL derived snapshot — customer-scoped facts (Dnt, open items, policies, identity tier) and conversation-scoped facts (phase, application). Phase is an input to predicates, not the exposure namespace; the catalog's per-phase tool tables are demoted to documentation grouping.
2. **Pinned DNT exposure predicates** (6-tool surface from #7): get_dnt_state — product in focus OR customer has any Dnt; get_dnt_questions — product type in focus or active session; get_dnt_next_question — active session; **open_dnt_session — (a) open application lacking valid DNT for its product type, OR (b) customer DNT expired/expiring within config window — renewal needs NO application** (engine picks update type, pre-filled); write_dnt_answer — active session + pending question; sign_dnt — session finished.
3. **Spec amendment:** catalog DNT "Exposed when" column rewritten to customer-scoped conditions; the Gherkin renewal scenario is satisfied without bending the application lifecycle.

— ALL 12 CROSS-TOPIC CONTRADICTIONS CLEARED (see entries above). —

### 2026-06-12 — M1 (CustomerProfile SSOT): RESOLVED — owned work package B0

Confirmed by user.

1. **New work package B0** (first of Block B, lands right after Block A, parallelizable with late A): merges the existing 2026-05-29 SSOT spec with T4 — per-field provenance store (declared|verified|conflict + source + evidence pointer); ONE CustomerProfile service as the only read/write path for profile facts; extractedProfile/CustomerInsight divergence retired into two-tier storage; age always derived (DOB → declaredAge precedence), never stored; **claim-and-merge primitive** (re-points Conversations/Dnt/Applications/ConsentEvents/evidence to the verified Customer; provenance-rule field merge — verified beats declared, newer declared beats older, conflicts surfaced; duplicate customer tombstoned — GDPR-relevant, feeds M3).
2. **Plan-wide ownership rule:** every customer-scoped aggregate keys on Customer.id and reads profile facts only via the service; no topic invents its own scoping or age/identity lookup. (Third single-source leg beside deriveAndExpose (#6) and evaluateEligibility (#9).)
3. **Sequencing:** B0 blocks dnt-sessions, application re-scoping, identity tools, consent backfill target.
4. **Documentation:** the 2026-05-29 SSOT spec is AMENDED with the provenance model — no second spec.

### 2026-06-12 — M2 (customer-scoped reads + re-engagement): RESOLVED

Confirmed by user.

1. Phase-entry circularity and channel questions: already dead via #10 (customer-scoped PAYMENT/POLICY predicates), #11 (channel indifference), #12 (full-snapshot predicates).
2. **Tool surface — 2 reads replace the catalog's 4:** `get_customer_profile` (kept name, re-backed by B0 service: profile + provenance + identity tier + history summary; replaces get_customer_info) and `get_open_items` (new). **get_application_list + get_quote_list dropped** (spec amendment; revisit only if a multi-product portfolio demands it).
3. **Open-item contract:** kinds = open/paused application · issued-unaccepted-unexpired quote · schedule with pending-due/failed installment · DNT expiring within config window · policy in PENDING_SUBMISSION/SUBMITTED. Shape = {kind, refId, age, nextAction} with **nextAction engine-derived and required to map to a currently-exposed tool** (briefing-integrity invariant applied to re-engagement).
4. **New build item — proactive re-engagement job v1** (narrow): triggers = abandoned payment after N days + quote nearing expiry (optionally expiring DNT); sends channel message with magic link that verifies AND returns to the conversation (fixes the dead post-payment magic-link URL, per T4-R5); verified-channel customers only; frequency caps; every outbound recorded as a ledger event. **Dunning excluded — M16.**

### 2026-06-12 — M3 (GDPR rights): RESOLVED — access + erasure on top of the #2 consent ledger

Confirmed by user. Consent capture/withdrawal/halt already resolved by contradiction #2.

1. **Pin:** withdrawal is scope-aware — withdraw(gdpr_processing) halts funnel commits (engine rule); withdraw(marketing) disables the M2 re-engagement job (job checks the consent ledger before every outbound).
2. **New build item — retention-policy table + erasure job:** per data class — legally retained (signed DNTs, policies, payments, consent records) ⇒ anonymize-what-is-allowed + retain-what-is-mandated, decision ledger-recorded; freely erasable (conversations, messages, insights, soft profile data of never-contracted customers) ⇒ full delete. Operator-approved execution (M5 queue). Pseudonymized-Customer tombstone aligns with B0 claim-and-merge. Existing app/api/gdpr/delete-data/route.ts gets audited and aligned under this table (plan review step).
3. **New build item (small) — data-access export:** dashboard/back-office delivery; the agent only takes the request (creates an operator work item); verified channel required (engine rule).
4. Retention durations per data class = config + **legal/compliance confirmation flag** (same pattern as free-look window).

### 2026-06-12 — M4 (GUI/uiAction swap-test parity): RESOLVED — GUI is the second client

Confirmed by user.

1. **Design rule:** synthetic actions (UI buttons) pass the FULL commit gateway (#8 sequence) with actor=gui — the action-adapter's unconditional execution dies in Block A. Swap test becomes mechanical; doubles as the missing defense-in-depth.
2. **Design rule:** the GUI renders from the same deriveAndExpose output the agent reads — available_actions ⇒ which buttons exist; blocked_actions ⇒ disabled affordances with the engine reason; requires_confirmation ⇒ confirm dialog carrying the signed token (GUI confirm submits the same commit + token the agent would). One exposure computation, two surfaces.
3. Domain renderers (show_question/show_quote/show_payment/new show_document_upload + OTP entry) survive as PRESENTATION of envelope/state data — never parallel truth.
4. **Ownership:** uiAction contract + adapter migration = explicit Block A item; renderer cleanup rides owning packages (show_policy_issued-at-accept dies with #5; payments adds ensure-payment-session renderer; identity adds upload/OTP).

### 2026-06-12 — M5 (operator/back-office surfaces): RESOLVED — WorkItem spine + operators through the gateway

Confirmed by user.

1. **New build item — generic WorkItem queue:** {kind, refs, status, priority, reason, createdBy, resolution, resolvedBy, timestamps}; kinds v1 = referral, escalation (escalate_to_human finally persists — replaces console.log), document_review, gdpr_erasure, gdpr_export, alert_flag. One queue, one admin list, kind-specific detail panels.
2. **Design rule:** operator decisions are commits through the same gateway (actor=operator): resolve_referral, mark_submitted, activate_policy(allianzPolicyNumber), approve_erasure… — same legality predicates (#5 transition table enforced), same envelope, same ledger. Free-form admin status edits die; who-moved-what-why audit comes free.
3. **Referred re-entry defined** (closes spec dead-end): generate_quote→referred ⇒ Application REFERRED + WorkItem(referral); blocked_actions explain "with underwriter"; approve ⇒ quote generation resumes and issues; reject ⇒ terminal with underwriter reason; customer notified via M2 machinery.
4. **Refund execution** = system effect of operator cancellation commits (free-look / pre-activation rejection per #5) → provider refund API → PaymentStatus.REFUNDED live, ledger-recorded.
5. **SOP steps become gateway commits** (mark_submitted, activate_policy incl. fixing the activation-email stub); manual shape preserved, properly recorded.

### 2026-06-12 — M6 (i18n): RESOLVED — the engine never speaks a human language

Confirmed by user.

1. **Design rule:** engine emits stable codes + structured params (blocked-action reasons, consequences, requires_identity.needs), never localized prose. The agent renders codes in the conversation language; the GUI renders via translations.ts keys per code. Ledger and test assertions stay language-independent.
2. **Schema rule:** all new authored customer-facing fields are bilingual {ro,en} (existing Question.text pattern); the ProductContent publish gate (T11.D2) refuses publication with a missing locale; EN-only features[] fixed in the T11.D5 content migration.
3. **Documents carry language:** Document registry rows record language; generation uses customer language; DisclosureAck records language + content version shown. RO-mandatory document list (IPID, terms?) flagged for legal confirmation; default stance RO authoritative, EN courtesy.
4. **Mid-conversation switch is presentation-only:** Conversation.language updates; zero engine-state effects (consequence of rule 1). Outbound messages (M2 re-engagement, activation email) use customer language.

### 2026-06-12 — M7 (suitability/demands-and-needs engine): RESOLVED — new engine, sibling of eligibility

Confirmed by user. Distinction pinned: eligibility = "may we sell this" (#9); suitability = "does it match the declared demands and needs" (IDD).

1. **New build item — suitability engine:** typed per-product demands-and-needs rules (DNT-answer facts → fit conditions) + pure `evaluateSuitability(rules, dntFacts) → {verdict: suitable|conditionally_suitable|unsuitable, mismatches:[{rule,reason}]}`, in the T12.D3 decision core beside evaluateEligibility.
2. **Three consumption points:** (a) post-sign_dnt verdict injected into DerivedState — deterministic input for recommendation + the consultative-pushback scenario; (b) generate_quote gate — compliance_block gets its source; mismatch ⇒ documented-warning flow via **SuitabilityWarningAck** commit (sibling of DisclosureAck; hard-block vs warn-and-allow = product config; unacknowledged mismatch blocks with reason); (c) **suitability report generated at quote issuance** (timing fix of lib/compliance/dnt-report.ts — was post-policy) from the same verdict, stored in the Document registry.
3. **Agent invariant:** fit claims engine-gated — never "this fits your needs" without a suitable verdict in state.
4. Rule content for protect = compliance/legal input flag; v1 mechanism + documented-warning trail is the deliverable.

### 2026-06-12 — M8 (observability/audit of the envelope): RESOLVED by absorption + three pins

Confirmed by user. ~90% absorbed by T14.D1/D2/D4 + contradiction #8 (ledger args-hash + stored outcome). Residual pins:

1. **Content-version stamps per turn:** TurnDebug snapshot records the ProductContent version id(s) injected into that turn's prompt — "which approved claim set was in force when the agent said X" answerable per turn (schema detail on T14.D2).
2. **Versioned, typed ConversationExport contract:** explicit schema version field + typed contract shared by drawer download, replay, and the T12.D4 assertion library.
3. **No TurnTrace schema change** — only #10 tolerant phase-name readers touch it.

### 2026-06-12 — M9 (migration & deploy sequencing): RESOLVED — plan backbone; DEMO DATA ONLY

Confirmed by user, with a decisive simplification: **all customer data is demo data — no real customers, no customer-data preservation required.**

1. M9 = the implementation plan's sequencing backbone, not a work package: every package carries its schema migrations; the plan gets a master ordering section.
2. Rules retained: schema-with-code packaging; **coupled flips land in one package** (policy-creation flip per #5; consent-truth flip per #2; conversation-status change per #11 — these matter for code-path consistency regardless of data); dead-config cleanup (Workflow*/skill-pack gating/phantom seeds) as its own late-Block-A package, after the legality engine replaces gating.
3. Rules SIMPLIFIED by demo-data reality: **no customer-data backfills** — DNT/consent/application re-key migrations may be destructive (drop + recreate); demo data is reset + reseeded (seed scripts updated instead of backfill scripts written). Historical TurnDebug/TurnTrace tolerant phase readers (#10) become optional — history is disposable; wipe is acceptable.
4. Draft new-table inventory (finalized in the plan): Dnt, DntSession, ConsentEvent, PaymentSchedule(+installments), webhook inbox, DisclosureAck, SuitabilityWarningAck, Document, ProductContent, commit ledger, WorkItem, VerificationChallenge, CustomerDocument/evidence, B0 provenance store. Enum changes: Quote (ISSUED/CANCELLED), Application (REFERRED + T5.D6 set), Policy (LAPSED), Conversation (ACTIVE/ARCHIVED). Plus protect content migration (T11.D5, bilingual fix) and seed cleanup.

### 2026-06-12 — M10 (outage/resilience semantics): RESOLVED — unavailable + pending added to the envelope

Confirmed by user.

1. **Envelope additions:** `unavailable` ({retryable, retryAfter?} — timeout/circuit-open/provider-down; **invariant: unavailable ≠ rejected** — state unchanged, agent may only narrate "couldn't complete, retry shortly", never an invented outcome) and `pending` (operation recorded, result unknown — external checks, settlement gaps).
2. The pending/referred generate_quote dead-end closes: application HOLDS (REFERRED per M5 or pending-check); generate_quote re-exposed by the engine when the check clears.
3. **Retry policy by kind:** reads — executor may retry, circuit breaker stays; commits — never auto-retried (idempotent replay #8 makes customer-driven resubmission the only retry); system effects — inbox/job machinery (T8.D3).
4. **Degraded-mode exposure:** circuit-breaker state is an input to deriveAndExpose; a known-down tool appears in blocked_actions as `temporarily_unavailable`; escalate_to_human always exposed as the floor.
5. **Spec amendments:** taxonomy += unavailable, pending; `pending_external_check` Examples row corrected from rejection to pending.

### 2026-06-12 — M12 (skill-pack subsystem fate): RESOLVED — retired, roles re-homed

Confirmed by user.

| Pack role | New home |
|---|---|
| Tool gating | Legality engine (T1.D3) |
| Prompt content | Per-(phase,subphase) sections map (T10.D4) for behavior; versioned ProductContent (T11.D2) for product selling content (governed, publish-gated, version-stamped per M8). Playbook prices die — prices only from the engine |
| Per-turn activation | Nothing — dead since gate retirement; phase-driven sections are deterministic |

1. **Delete** SkillPack model + skill-pack-loader.ts + seeds + pack-contract tests, inside the M9 dead-config cleanup package (late Block A, after legality engine owns gating).
2. **Mandatory salvage-audit first:** review the five seeded packs' guidance text; port what is still true into phase sections / ProductContent (feeds M13).
3. Rejected alternative: packs as a second prompt-CMS — recreates the dual-truth/drift pattern the transformation kills elsewhere.

### 2026-06-12 — M13 (conversational-pathology preservation): RESOLVED — acceptance criteria on the sections rework

Confirmed by user.

1. **T10.D4 acceptance criteria:** (a) behavioral-content inventory of every shipped prompt section BEFORE any rework, each rule tagged with the pathology/scenario it serves; (b) old-section → new-(phase,subphase) mapping; (c) **no content dropped without an explicit "retired because X" note**; (d) the four pathology verify scripts (scripts/verify-pathology1..4.ts) green before AND after the rework.
2. Pathology checks migrate into the T12.D4 recorded-assertion layer and the end-of-plan triage catalog (deflection loop = repeated_assistant_message-class check, proven in the removed prototype).
3. **Prompt-vs-mechanism hierarchy:** pathologies gaining mechanical guards (deflection→funnel_stalled monitor; tool-narration→detector + envelope confirmations; empty-category→catalog overview + engine-grounded exposure; permission-asking→largely dissolved by engine-computed availability) can afford lighter prompt language; those without stay load-bearing prose, ported near-verbatim.

### 2026-06-12 — M14/M15/M16: EXPLICIT DEFERS with un-defer triggers

Confirmed by user. Out of build scope, recorded so nothing is silently forgotten:

- **M14 (parallel candidate products): DEFERRED.** Single candidateProductId pointer + candidate-SSOT regression guard stay normative; compare_products stays a stateless read. **Trigger: a second product lands in the catalog** (then a small design question inside the product-data package).
- **M15 (answer freshness + duplicate-policy detection): DEFERRED.** Re-application freshness already covered by T5.D5 prefill-as-proposals; staleness window for resumed applications deferred — **trigger: real customers**. Duplicate-policy detection requires a CNP blind index (random-IV encryption forbids equality lookup) — blind index recorded as optional add-on inside the identity package; the business rule itself deferred — **trigger: production launch / multi-policy portfolio**.
- **M16 (dunning/grace/lapse): rules DEFERRED, substrate already decided** (per-installment schedule T8.D1; LAPSED in the policy machine T9.D3; M2 re-engagement as channel; #5 refund mechanics). Deferred content = grace length, retry cadence, reinstatement — legal/business input. **Trigger: real recurring payments live.**
